<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Alternative_forms">Alternative forms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=football&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Alternative forms">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/foot-ball#English" title="foot-ball">foot-ball</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/foot_ball#English" title="foot ball">foot ball</a></span> (<i>dated</i>)</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=football&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/footbal#Middle_English" title="footbal">footbal</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/foteball#Middle_English" title="foteball">foteball</a></i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/foot#English" title="foot">foot</a></i> +‎ <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/ball#English" title="ball">ball</a></i>, which may refer to the act of kicking a ball with the feet. The name for the briefcase is a play on “dropkick”, the code name of an early version of the nuclear war plan.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=football&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Pronunciation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/General_American" class="extiw" title="w:General American">General American</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/ˈfʊtbɔl/</span>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">[ˈfʊʔtbɔɫ]</span>, <span class="IPA">[ˈfʊʔt̚bɔɫ]</span></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Received_Pronunciation" class="extiw" title="w:Received Pronunciation">Received Pronunciation</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/ˈfʊtbɔːl/</span>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">[ˈfʊʔt̚bɔːl]</span>, <span class="IPA">[ˈfʊʔtʰbɔːl]</span>, <span class="IPA">[ˈfʊʔbɔːl]</span></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Canadian_English" class="extiw" title="w:Canadian English">Canada</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/ˈfʊtbɑl/</span>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">[fʷʊʔt̚bɑɫ]</span></li></ul></li>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=football&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">football</strong> (<i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#countable" title="Appendix:Glossary">countable</a> and <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/footballs#English" title="footballs">footballs</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">general</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A sport played <a href="/wiki/on_foot" title="on foot">on foot</a> in which teams attempt to get a ball into a <a href="/wiki/goal" title="goal">goal</a> or <a href="/wiki/zone" title="zone">zone</a> defended by the other team.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Roman and medieval <b>football</b> matches were more violent than any modern type of <b>football</b>.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_Kingdom" class="extiw" title="w:United Kingdom">UK</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/association_football" title="association football">Association football</a>: a <a href="/wiki/game" title="game">game</a> in which two <a href="/wiki/team" title="team">teams</a> each contend to get a <a href="/wiki/round" title="round">round</a> <a href="/wiki/ball" title="ball">ball</a> into the other team's <a href="/wiki/goal" title="goal">goal</a> primarily by <a href="/wiki/kick" title="kick">kicking</a> the ball. Known as <a href="/wiki/soccer" title="soccer">soccer</a> in Canada, the United States, Australia, and New Zealand.
<span class="HQToggle" style="margin-left: 5px;"><a>synonym&nbsp;▲</a></span><dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <i>see</i> <a href="/wiki/Thesaurus:football" title="Thesaurus:football">Thesaurus:<span class="Latn" lang="en">football</span></a></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Each team scored three goals when they played <b>football</b>.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/American_football" title="American football">American football</a>: a <a href="/wiki/game" title="game">game</a> played on a field of 100 yards long and 53 1/3 yards wide in which two teams of 11 players attempt to get an <a href="/wiki/ovoid" title="ovoid">ovoid</a> ball to the end of each other's territory.
<span class="HQToggle" style="margin-left: 5px;"><a>synonym&nbsp;▲</a></span><dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <i>see</i> <a href="/wiki/Thesaurus:football" title="Thesaurus:football">Thesaurus:<span class="Latn" lang="en">football</span></a></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Each team scored two touchdowns when they played <b>football</b>.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Canada" class="extiw" title="w:Canada">Canada</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Canadian_football" title="Canadian football">Canadian football</a>: a <a href="/wiki/game" title="game">game</a> played on a field of 110 yards long and 65 yards wide in which two teams of 12 players attempt to get an <a href="/wiki/ovoid" title="ovoid">ovoid</a> ball to the end of each other's territory.
<span class="HQToggle" style="margin-left: 5px;"><a>synonym&nbsp;▲</a></span><dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <i>see</i> <a href="/wiki/Thesaurus:football" title="Thesaurus:football">Thesaurus:<span class="Latn" lang="en">football</span></a></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">They played <b>football</b> in the snow.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Australia" class="extiw" title="w:Australia">Australia</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> Victoria<span class="ib-comma">,</span> South Australia<span class="ib-comma">,</span> Western Australia<span class="ib-comma">,</span> Tasmania<span class="ib-comma">,</span> Northern Territory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Australian_rules_football" title="Australian rules football">Australian rules football</a>.
<span class="HQToggle" style="margin-left: 5px;"><a>synonym&nbsp;▲</a></span><dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <i>see</i> <a href="/wiki/Thesaurus:football" title="Thesaurus:football">Thesaurus:<span class="Latn" lang="en">football</span></a></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ireland" class="extiw" title="w:Ireland">Ireland</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Gaelic_football" title="Gaelic football">Gaelic football</a>: a field game played with similar rules to <a href="/wiki/hurling" title="hurling">hurling</a>, but using hands and feet rather than a stick, and a ball, similar to, yet smaller than a soccer ball.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Australia" class="extiw" title="w:Australia">Australia</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> New South Wales<span class="ib-comma">,</span> Queensland<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/rugby_league" title="rugby league">rugby league</a>.
<span class="HQToggle" style="margin-left: 5px;"><a>synonym&nbsp;▲</a></span><dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <i>see</i> <a href="/wiki/Thesaurus:football" title="Thesaurus:football">Thesaurus:<span class="Latn" lang="en">football</span></a></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Australia" class="extiw" title="w:Australia">Australia</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ireland" class="extiw" title="w:Ireland">Ireland</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Zealand" class="extiw" title="w:New Zealand">New Zealand</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/rugby_union" title="rugby union">rugby union</a>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#countable" title="Appendix:Glossary">countable</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The ball used in any game called "football".
<span class="HQToggle" style="margin-left: 5px;"><a>synonym&nbsp;▲</a></span><dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <i>see</i> <a href="/wiki/Thesaurus:football" title="Thesaurus:football">Thesaurus:<span class="Latn" lang="en">football</span></a></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">The player kicked the <b>football</b>.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Practice of these particular games, or techniques used in them.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#figurative" title="Appendix:Glossary">figuratively</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#countable" title="Appendix:Glossary">countable</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An item of discussion, particularly in a back-and-forth manner
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">That budget item became a political <b>football</b>.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a> <a href="/wiki/military" title="military">military</a> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#slang" title="Appendix:Glossary">slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#countable" title="Appendix:Glossary">countable</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The leather <a href="/wiki/briefcase" title="briefcase">briefcase</a> containing classified nuclear war plans which is always near the US President.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><span class="HQToggle" style="margin-left: 5px;"><a>synonyms&nbsp;▲</a></span><span class="HQToggle" style="margin-left: 5px;"><a>coordinate term&nbsp;▼</a></span><dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/w/index.php?title=nuclear_football&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="nuclear football (page does not exist)">nuclear football</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/w/index.php?title=atomic_football&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="atomic football (page does not exist)">atomic football</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/black_box#English" title="black box">black box</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/black_bag#English" title="black bag">black bag</a></span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms coordinate-term" style="display: none;"><span class="defdate">Coordinate term:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/Cheget#English" title="Cheget">Cheget</a></span></span></dd></dl>
<ul style="display: none;"><li><b>1994</b>, Herbert L. Abrams, <i>The President Has Been Shot: Confusion, Disability, and the 25th Amendment</i>, Stanford University Press (<a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/9780804723251" title="Special:BookSources/9780804723251">→ISBN</a>), <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=DP_IW4Zmi9YC&amp;lpg=PA126&amp;dq=president%20%22football%22&amp;pg=PA126#v=onepage&amp;q=president%20%22football%22&amp;f=false">page 126</a>:
<dl><dd>The aide rides, along with the president's physician, in the “control car,” third in line in the motorcade. He is responsible for the <b>football</b> (or “black box” or “black bag”), a briefcase containing the codes and targeting information the president would require to order or authorize a nuclear attack.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2020</b> June 23,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Bolton" class="extiw" title="w:John Bolton">John Bolton</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Room_Where_It_Happened" class="extiw" title="w:The Room Where It Happened">The Room Where It Happened: A White House Memoir</a></cite>, New York, N.Y.: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Simon_%26_Schuster" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Simon &amp; Schuster">Simon &amp; Schuster</a>, <small><a href="/wiki/Special:BookSources/978-1-9821-4803-4" title="Special:BookSources/978-1-9821-4803-4">→ISBN</a></small>, page 155:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">After the lunch broke, we walked to the Trump-Putin press conference, which started about 6 p.m.  As Kelly observed to me at some point, there were now two military aides in the room, each carrying his country's nuclear <b>football</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=football&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Usage notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>In the US the term 'football' is used in almost all contexts to mean <a href="/wiki/American_Football" title="American Football">American Football</a>, contrary to the rest of the English speaking world who call 'Association Football' (<a href="/wiki/soccer" title="soccer">soccer</a>) football.
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=football&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Verb">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">football</strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3|s|pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/footballs#English" title="footballs">footballs</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres|ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/footballing#English" title="footballing">footballing</a></b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past|and|past|ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/footballed#English" title="footballed">footballed</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#intransitive" title="Appendix:Glossary">intransitive</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#rare" title="Appendix:Glossary">rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To play football.
<span class="HQToggle"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><b>1969</b>, Alec Hugh Chisholm, <i>The Joy of the Earth</i> (page 358)
<dl><dd>It was an announcement of the outbreak of what is now termed World War I. Some of us lads were <b>footballing</b> when we heard the news. It left us bewildered.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2019</b>, David Randall, <i>Suburbia: A Far from Ordinary Place</i>
<dl><dd>You walked up our road, passed the elms that bordered our park until Dutch disease killed them in the early 1970s, diagonally crossed its field where we <b>footballed</b>, turned right at the drinking fountain and cattle trough <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Interlingua">Interlingua</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=football&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Interlingua">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=football&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=football&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="enm">football</strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Alternative form of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href="/wiki/foteball#Middle_English" title="foteball">foteball</a></i></span></span></li></ol>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Portuguese">Portuguese</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=football&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Portuguese">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=football&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Noun">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="pt">football</strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Dated spelling of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="pt"><a href="/wiki/futebol#Portuguese" title="futebol">futebol</a></i></span></span>.</li></ol>
<hr>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Swedish">Swedish</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=football&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Swedish">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=football&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/football#English" title="football">football</a></i>, clipping of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/American_football#English" title="American football">American football</a></i>,.
</p><p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="sv">football</strong>&nbsp;<span class="gender"><abbr title="common gender">c</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><a href="/wiki/American_football" title="American football">American football</a></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=football&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Usage notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Found primarily in subtitling of television and movies, due to its brevity, where <a href="/wiki/fotboll" title="fotboll">fotboll</a> could be interpreted as <a href="/wiki/association_football" title="association football">association football</a>.
</p>
